update_state_57_names={
	57={
		if ={ 
			limit = { CONTROLLER={ is_ukraine_tag = yes } }
			set_state_name = STATE_57_UKR
		}
		else_if ={ 
			limit = { CONTROLLER={ is_russia_tag = yes } }
			set_state_name = STATE_57_SOV
		}
		else_if={
			limit = { CONTROLLER={ is_poland_tag = yes } }
			set_state_name = STATE_57_POL
		}
		else ={ 
			reset_state_name = yes
		}
	}
	if={
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 11433 is_ukraine_tag = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 11433 name = VICTORY_POINTS_11433_UKR }
	}
	else_if={
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 11433 is_russia_tag = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 11433 name = VICTORY_POINTS_11433_SOV }
	}
	else_if={
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 11433 is_poland_tag = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 11433 name = VICTORY_POINTS_11433_POL }
	}
	else={
		reset_province_name = 11433
	}
}

		}
		else ={ 
			reset_state_name = yes
		}
	}
	
	if={
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 6310 OR={ original_tag = UKR is_puppet_of = UKR original_tag = SOV is_puppet_of = SOV } } }
		set_province_name = { id = 6310 name = VICTORY_POINTS_6310_UKR }
	}
	else_if={
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 6310 is_poland_tag = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 6310 name = VICTORY_POINTS_6310_POL }
	}
	else={
		reset_province_name = 6310

		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 9390 OR={ original_tag = UKR is_puppet_of = UKR original_tag = SOV is_puppet_of = SOV } } }

update_state_73_names={
	73={
		if ={ 
			limit = { CONTROLLER={ is_ukraine_tag = yes } }
			set_state_name = STATE_73_UKR
		}

		}
		else_if={
			limit = { CONTROLLER={ is_poland_tag = yes } }
			set_state_name = STATE_73_POL
		}
		else ={ 
			reset_state_name = yes
		}
	}
	
	if={
		limit = { has_global_flag = UKRAINE_CITIES_RENAMED_FLAG }
		if={
			limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 3744 is_poland_tag = yes } }
			set_province_name = { id = 3744 name = VICTORY_POINTS_3744_POL_RENAMED }
		}
		else_if={
			limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 3744 is_russia_tag = yes } }
			set_province_name = { id = 3744 name = VICTORY_POINTS_3744_SOV_RENAMED }
		}
		else={
			set_province_name = { id = 3744 name = VICTORY_POINTS_3744_RENAMED }
		}
	}
	else={
		if={
			limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 3744 is_ukraine_tag = yes } }
			set_province_name = { id = 3744 name = VICTORY_POINTS_3744_UKR }
		}
		else_if={
			limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 3744 is_russia_tag = yes } }
			set_province_name = { id = 3744 name = VICTORY_POINTS_3744_SOV }
		}
		else_if={
			limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 3744 is_poland_tag = yes } }
			set_province_name = { id = 3744 name = VICTORY_POINTS_3744_POL }
		}
		else={
			reset_province_name = 3744
		}
	}
	
	if={
		limit = { any_country = { controls_province = 16999 is_ukraine_tag = yes } }
		set_province_name = { id = 16999 name = VICTORY_POINTS_16999_UKR }
	}
	else_if={
